-- Auto Teleport + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura (Receiver)
local autoReceiverGeneral = false
local receiverGeneralLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverGeneral = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverGeneral = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverGeneralLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverGeneralLoop)
                receiverGeneralLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverGeneralLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoReceiverGeneral do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralAbility (every 0.1 seconds)
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverGeneralLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverGeneralLoop)
                receiverGeneralLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Defense",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3-4 Quest"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura (Receiver)
local autoReceiverBarrier = false
local receiverBarrierLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverBarrier = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverBarrier = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverBarrierLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverBarrierLoop)
                receiverBarrierLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverBarrierLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoReceiverBarrier do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- Barrier ability (every 0.01 seconds)
                        local barrier = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Barrier")
                        if barrier then
                            barrier:FireServer(1)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.01)
                        
                        -- DefenseHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local defenseHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("DefenseHit")
                        if defenseHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        defenseHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Barrier + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverBarrierLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverBarrierLoop)
                receiverBarrierLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Mace",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura (Receiver)
local autoReceiverSlapAura = false
local receiverSlapAuraLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverSlapAura = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverSlapAura = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverSlapAuraLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSlapAuraLoop)
                receiverSlapAuraLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverSlapAuraLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoReceiverSlapAura do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart, 93.05674743652344)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverSlapAuraLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSlapAuraLoop)
                receiverSlapAuraLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll (Helper)
local autoHelperRagdoll = false
local helperRagdollLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoHelperRagdoll = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoHelperRagdoll = false
                return
            end
            
            if helperRagdollLoop then
                task.cancel(helperRagdollLoop)
                helperRagdollLoop = nil
            end
            
            helperRagdollLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoHelperRagdoll do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        -- Wait for character if dead
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            print("⏳ Waiting for respawn...")
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Check if player has entered
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        -- Auto Enter Arena
                        if not hasEntered then
                            print("🚶 Entering arena...")
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        else
                            print("✅ Already in arena")
                        end
                        
                        -- Teleport to Receiver position
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Check Ragdolled
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            print("💀 Died due to ragdoll!")
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if helperRagdollLoop then
                task.cancel(helperRagdollLoop)
                helperRagdollLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Killstreak",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quest"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura (Receiver)
local autoReceiverSlapAura = false
local receiverSlapAuraLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverSlapAura = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverSlapAura = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverSlapAuraLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSlapAuraLoop)
                receiverSlapAuraLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverSlapAuraLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoReceiverSlapAura do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- KSHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local ksHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("KSHit")
                        if ksHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        ksHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverSlapAuraLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSlapAuraLoop)
                receiverSlapAuraLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

local Tab = Window:MakeTab({

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability (Receiver)
local autoReceiverSentry = false
local receiverSentryLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverSentry = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverSentry = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverSentryLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSentryLoop)
                receiverSentryLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverSentryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local abilityTimer = 0
                
                while autoReceiverSentry do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- Sentry ability (every 6 seconds)
                        abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                        if abilityTimer >= 6 then
                            abilityTimer = 0
                            local sentry = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Sentry")
                            if sentry then
                                sentry:FireServer()
                                print("🔫 Sentry ability used!")
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Sentry Ability Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverSentryLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSentryLoop)
                receiverSentryLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

    Name = "Helper"

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver/Sentry's Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll (Helper)
local autoHelperSentry = false
local helperSentryLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver/Sentry's Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoHelperSentry = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoHelperSentry = false
                return
            end
            
            if helperSentryLoop then
                task.cancel(helperSentryLoop)
                helperSentryLoop = nil
            end
            
            helperSentryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoHelperSentry do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        -- Wait for character if dead
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            print("⏳ Waiting for respawn...")
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Check if player has entered
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        -- Auto Enter Arena
                        if not hasEntered then
                            print("🚶 Entering arena...")
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        else
                            print("✅ Already in arena")
                        end
                        
                        -- Teleport to Receiver position (Safespot)
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Find Turret and teleport to Glove
                        local turret = workspace:FindFirstChild("Turret")
                        if turret then
                            local hingePart = turret:FindFirstChild("HingePart")
                            if hingePart then
                                local glove = hingePart:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                                if glove then
                                    hrp.CFrame = glove.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                    print("🎯 Teleported to Sentry's Glove!")
                                else
                                    print("⚠️ Glove not found in Turret.HingePart")
                                end
                            else
                                print("⚠️ HingePart not found in Turret")
                            end
                        else
                            print("⚠️ Turret not found in workspace")
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Check Ragdolled
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            print("💀 Died due to ragdoll!")
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if helperSentryLoop then
                task.cancel(helperSentryLoop)
                helperSentryLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Wormhole",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quest"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura + Auto Teleport To Circle Portals (Receiver)
local autoReceiverWormhole = false
local receiverWormholeLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura + Auto Teleport To Circle Portals",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverWormhole = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverWormhole = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverWormholeLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverWormholeLoop)
                receiverWormholeLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverWormholeLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local portalTimer = 0
                
                while autoReceiverWormhole do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- WormholePlace ability (every 0.1 seconds)
                        local wormholePlace = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("WormholePlace")
                        if wormholePlace then
                            wormholePlace:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        -- WormHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local wormHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("WormHit")
                        if wormHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        wormHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- Auto Teleport to Circle Portals (every 2 seconds)
                        portalTimer = portalTimer + 0.5
                        if portalTimer >= 2 then
                            portalTimer = 0
                            
                            local wormholes = workspace:FindFirstChild("Wormholes")
                            if wormholes then
                                local one = wormholes:FindFirstChild("One")
                                local two = wormholes:FindFirstChild("Two")
                                
                                if one and two and hrp then
                                    -- Alternate between One and Two
                                    if portalTimer == 0 then
                                        hrp.CFrame = one.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                        print("🌀 Teleported to Wormhole One")
                                    else
                                        hrp.CFrame = two.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                        print("🌀 Teleported to Wormhole Two")
                                    end
                                else
                                    print("⚠️ Wormholes folder or parts not found!")
                                end
                            else
                                print("⚠️ Wormholes folder not found!")
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Wormhole Ability + Slap Aura + Portal Teleport Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverWormholeLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverWormholeLoop)
                receiverWormholeLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

    Name = "Helper"
})

local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Cherry",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3-4 Quest"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura + Auto Use Ability + Auto Use Cherry's Clone Glove (Receiver)
local autoReceiverCherry = false
local receiverCherryLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura + Auto Use Ability + Auto Use Cherry's Clone Glove",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverCherry = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverCherry = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverCherryLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverCherryLoop)
                receiverCherryLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverCherryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local cloneTimer = 0
                
                while autoReceiverCherry do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralAbility (every 0.1 seconds)
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- Auto Use Cherry's Clone Glove (every 0.5 seconds)
                        cloneTimer = cloneTimer + 0.5
                        if cloneTimer >= 0.5 then
                            cloneTimer = 0
                            
                            local cherryStorage = workspace:FindFirstChild("cherry_storage")
                            if cherryStorage then
                                for _, model in pairs(cherryStorage:GetChildren()) do
                                    if model:IsA("Model") and model.Name:lower():match("cherry") then
                                        local cloneRemote = model:FindFirstChild("clone_remote")
                                        if cloneRemote then
                                            pcall(function()
                                                cloneRemote:FireServer()
                                                print("🍒 Cherry clone remote fired!")
                                            end)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Slap Aura + Ability + Cherry Clone Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverCherryLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverCherryLoop)
                receiverCherryLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Cherry's Clone Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll (Helper)
local autoHelperCherry = false
local helperCherryLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Teleport To Cherry's Clone Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoHelperCherry = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoHelperCherry = false
                return
            end
            
            if helperCherryLoop then
                task.cancel(helperCherryLoop)
                helperCherryLoop = nil
            end
            
            helperCherryLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoHelperCherry do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        -- Wait for character if dead
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            print("⏳ Waiting for respawn...")
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Check if player has entered
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        -- Auto Enter Arena
                        if not hasEntered then
                            print("🚶 Entering arena...")
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        else
                            print("✅ Already in arena")
                        end
                        
                        -- Teleport to Receiver position (Safespot)
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Find Cherry's Clone Glove
                        local cherryStorage = workspace:FindFirstChild("cherry_storage")
                        if cherryStorage then
                            for _, model in pairs(cherryStorage:GetChildren()) do
                                if model:IsA("Model") and model.Name:lower():match("cherry") then
                                    local tool = model:FindFirstChild("Cherry")
                                    if tool then
                                        local glove = tool:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                                        if glove and glove:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                            hrp.CFrame = glove.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                            print("🍒 Teleported to Cherry's Clone Glove!")
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        else
                            print("⚠️ cherry_storage folder not found!")
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Check Ragdolled
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            print("💀 Died due to ragdoll!")
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Cherry Clone Glove + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if helperCherryLoop then
                task.cancel(helperCherryLoop)
                helperCherryLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

end

                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- BONK ability (every 0.1 seconds)
                        local bonk = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BONK")
                        if bonk then
                            bonk:FireServer(-0.2956634000001941)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + BONK Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverBonkLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverBonkLoop)
                receiverBonkLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll (Helper)
local autoHelperBonk = false
local helperBonkLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoHelperBonk = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoHelperBonk = false
                return
            end
            
            if helperBonkLoop then
                task.cancel(helperBonkLoop)
                helperBonkLoop = nil
            end
            
            helperBonkLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoHelperBonk do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        -- Wait for character if dead
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            print("⏳ Waiting for respawn...")
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Check if player has entered
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        -- Auto Enter Arena
                        if not hasEntered then
                            print("🚶 Entering arena...")
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        else
                            print("✅ Already in arena")
                        end
                        
                        -- Teleport to Receiver position (Safespot)
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Check Ragdolled
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            print("💀 Died due to ragdoll!")
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Auto Die On Ragdoll Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if helperBonkLoop then
                task.cancel(helperBonkLoop)
                helperBonkLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

end

local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Cloud",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-4 Quest (SOON REWORK)"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "2 Quest"
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Safespot",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local character = player.Character
        
        -- Check conditions
        local hasSpinGlove = player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud"
        local hasEntered = character and character:FindFirstChild("entered")
        local hasSafespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
        
        if not hasSpinGlove or not hasEntered or not hasSafespot then
            local errorMsg = ""
            if not hasSpinGlove then
                errorMsg = "Equip Spin Glove"
            elseif not hasEntered then
                errorMsg = "Enter Arena First"
            elseif not hasSafespot then
                errorMsg = "Create Safespot First"
            end
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = errorMsg,
                Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        -- Teleport to Safespot
        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
        if safespot then
            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
            if base then
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if hrp then
                    hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                    
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Teleported",
                        Content = "Teleported to Safespot!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                        Time = 2
                    })
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "3 Quest"
})

Tab:AddSlider({
    Name = "Set Speed Cloud",
    Min = 0.1,
    Max = 1.2,
    Default = 0.5,
    Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
    Increment = 0.1,
    ValueName = "Speed",
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.SetSpeedCloud = Value
    end
})

CloudSpeed = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Set Cloud Speed",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.CloudSpeed = Value

        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud" then
            while _G.CloudSpeed and game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Cloud" do
                for i, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                    if v.Name:match(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name) and v:FindFirstChild("BodyVelocity") then
                        v.BodyVelocity.Velocity = v.BodyVelocity.Velocity * _G.SetSpeedCloud
                    end
                end
                task.wait(0.10)
            end
        elseif _G.CloudSpeed == true then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Cloud",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 5
            })
            wait(0.05)
            CloudSpeed:Set(false)
        end
    end
})

end

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura (Receiver)
local autoReceiverSoul = false
local receiverSoulLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverSoul = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverSoul = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverSoulLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSoulLoop)
                receiverSoulLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverSoulLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoReceiverSoul do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralAbility (every 0.1 seconds)
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer(false)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        -- Soul charge remote (every 0.1 seconds)
                        local soulRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Events")
                        if soulRemote then
                            local soul = soulRemote:FindFirstChild("soul")
                            if soul then
                                soul:FireServer("charge")
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Soul Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverSoulLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverSoulLoop)
                receiverSoulLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Teleport to Pocket Dimension Portal (WellModel)
                        local wellModel = workspace:FindFirstChild("WellModel")
                        if wellModel then
                            local part = wellModel:FindFirstChild("Part")
                            if part and part:IsA("BasePart") then
                                hrp.CFrame = part.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)

                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Check if player has entered
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        -- Auto Enter Arena
                        if not hasEntered then
                            print("🚶 Entering arena...")
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        else
                            print("✅ Already in arena")
                        end
                        
                        -- Teleport to Receiver position (Safespot)
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        -- Teleport to BusModel
                        local busModel = workspace:FindFirstChild("BusModel")
                        if busModel and busModel:IsA("MeshPart") then
                            hrp.CFrame = busModel.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                            print("🚌 Teleported to Bus!")
                        else
                            -- If BusModel not found, search for any MeshPart named BusModel
                            local found = false
                            for _, obj in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
                                if obj:IsA("MeshPart") and obj.Name == "BusModel" then
                                    hrp.CFrame = obj.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                    found = true
                                    print("🚌 Teleported to Bus (found in descendants)!")
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                            if not found then
                                print("⚠️ BusModel not found in workspace!")
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Bus Teleport Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if helperBusLoop then
                task.cancel(helperBusLoop)
                helperBusLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura (Receiver)
local autoReceiverPhase = false
local receiverPhaseLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiverPhase = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                autoReceiverPhase = false
                return
            end
            
            if receiverPhaseLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverPhaseLoop)
                receiverPhaseLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverPhaseLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local abilityTimer = 0
                
                while autoReceiverPhase do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                -- Teleport to Safespot
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- PhaseA ability (every 14 seconds)
                        abilityTimer = abilityTimer + 0.5
                        if abilityTimer >= 14 then
                            abilityTimer = 0
                            local phaseA = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhaseA")
                            if phaseA then
                                phaseA:FireServer()
                                print("🌀 PhaseA ability used!")
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- PhaseH Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local phaseH = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("PhaseH")
                        if phaseH then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        phaseH:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Phase Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if receiverPhaseLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverPhaseLoop)
                receiverPhaseLoop = nil
            end
            
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Bomb",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-3 Quest"
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            -- START
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            
            -- Check if Bomb glove is equipped
            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value ~= "Bomb" then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Bomb Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            -- Check if Safespot exists
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Create Safespot first!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop = true
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        -- Wait for character if dead
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            print("⏳ Waiting for respawn...")
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Check if player has entered
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        -- Auto Enter Arena
                        if not hasEntered then
                            print("🚶 Entering arena...")
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(1)
                        else
                            print("✅ Already in arena")
                        end
                        
                        -- Teleport to Safespot
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                print("📍 Teleported to Safespot")
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        task.wait(1)
                        
                        -- Check Ragdolled before continuing
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            print("💀 Died due to ragdoll!")
                            task.wait(1)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Throw Bomb
                        local bombThrow = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("BombThrow")
                        if bombThrow then
                            bombThrow:FireServer("Ebutton")
                            print("💣 Bomb thrown!")
                        end
                        task.wait(1)
                        
                        -- Wait to teleport to bomb
                        local bombFound = false
                        for i = 1, 30 do -- Timeout after 30 seconds
                            if not getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop then break end
                            
                            for _, v in pairs(game.Workspace:GetChildren()) do
                                if v.Name and string.find(v.Name, "_bømb") then
                                    hrp.CFrame = v.CFrame
                                    bombFound = true
                                    print("💣 Teleported to bomb!")
                                    break
                                end
                            end
                            
                            if bombFound then
                                break
                            else
                                task.wait(1)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- Check Ragdolled after bomb teleport
                        ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            print("💀 Died due to ragdoll!")
                            task.wait(1)
                            return
                        end
                        
                        -- Kill player to reset
                        if humanoid then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            print("💀 Player killed to reset cycle")
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Bomb Tasks",
                Content = "Started! Teleporting to Safespot + Using Bomb",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            -- STOP
            getgenv().AutoBombTasksLoop = false
            
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})
