Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Use Bubble's Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            -- START
            
            getgenv().AutoBubbleLoop = true
            task.spawn(function()
                while getgenv().AutoBubbleLoop do
                    game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").BubbleThrow:FireServer()
                    task.wait(10)
                end
            end)
        else
            -- STOP
            getgenv().AutoBubbleLoop = false
            
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Bubble Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Bubble" then
-- Get the ReplicatedStorage and Players service
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

-- Start the infinite loop to fire for all players
while true do
    -- Loop through each player in the game
    for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        -- Ensure the player has a character and it contains the "Right Arm"
        if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") then
            -- Create the arguments table for the FireServer function
            local args = {
                [1] = player.Character["Right Arm"]
            }

            -- Fire the server with the "Right Arm" part as an argument
            ReplicatedStorage.BubbleHit:FireServer(unpack(args))
        end
    end

    -- Wait 1 second before running the loop again (adjust the wait time as needed)
    task.wait(0.5)
end
else
OrionLib:MakeNotification({Name = "Error",Content = "Equip Bubble",Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",Time = 3})
end
end
})

end

    Default = false,

        if Value then
            -- Start the loop with exact 0.1 second interval
            shardCloneLoop = true
            
            spawn(function()
                while cherryCloneLoop do
                    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

                    if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Shard" then

                            Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                            Time = 3
                        })
                        wait(1) -- Wait longer when wrong glove
                    end
                    
                    wait(0.1) -- Normal 0.1 second delay
                end
            end)
        else
            -- Stop the loop
            shardCloneLoop = false
        end
    end
})

                local character = player.Character
                if character then
                    local leftArm = character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")
                    if leftArm then
                        replicatedStorage.ShardHIT:FireServer(leftArm)
                    end
                end
            end

            wait(0.5)
        end
    end

do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Moon",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quest"

Section = Tab:AddSection({

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Ragdoll + Auto Equip/Unequip Glove + Slap Aura
local moonGloveLoop = nil
local moonSlapLoop = nil
local moonRagdollLoop = nil
local moonToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Ragdoll + Auto Equip/Unequip Glove + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        moonToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            -- Teleport to Safespot loop
            task.spawn(function()
                while moonToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            -- Auto Ragdoll (every 0.1 seconds)
            moonRagdollLoop = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not moonToggle then return end
                pcall(function()
                    if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("entered") then
                        game.ReplicatedStorage.SelfKnockback:FireServer({
                            ["Force"] = 0,
                            ["Direction"] = Vector3.new(0, 0.01, 0)
                        })
                    end
                end)
            end)
            
            -- Auto Equip/Unequip Glove (every 0.1 seconds)
            moonGloveLoop = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                if not moonToggle then return end
                pcall(function()
                    local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                    local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
                    local character = player.Character
                    
                    if backpack and character then
                        local moonTool = backpack:FindFirstChild("Moon") or character:FindFirstChild("Moon")
                        if moonTool then
                            local currentlyEquipped = character:FindFirstChild("Moon")
                            if currentlyEquipped then
                                moonTool.Parent = backpack
                            else
                                moonTool.Parent = character
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end)
            
            -- CelestialHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
            task.spawn(function()
                while moonToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local celestialHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CelestialHit")
                        if celestialHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        celestialHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Moon",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ragdoll + Equip/Unequip + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            if moonRagdollLoop then
                moonRagdollLoop:Disconnect()
                moonRagdollLoop = nil
            end
            if moonGloveLoop then
                moonGloveLoop:Disconnect()
                moonGloveLoop = nil
            end
            moonToggle = false
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)

            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura
local rageToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        rageToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while rageToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GRRRRR ability (every 0.1 seconds)
                        local grrrr = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GRRRRR")
                        if grrrr then
                            grrrr:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.1)
                        
                        -- GRRRR Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local grrrrHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GRRRR")
                        if grrrrHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        grrrrHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Rage",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                else
                                    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

-- Auto teleport to safespot position
Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "2 Quest"
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Place Tycoon To Safe Spot",
    Callback = function()
        if game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Tycoon" then
            local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local hrp = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            
            if not hrp then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Character not found!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return
            end

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
            task.wait(1)

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(17884, -24, -3539)
            task.wait(1)

            local args = {
                [1] = CFrame.new(17893.552734375, -26.257728576660156, -3535.35888671875, 
                0.00862560048699379, 3.3499091500743816e-08, -0.9999628067016602, 
                8.43312697451637e-10, 1, 3.350761090814558e-08, 
                0.9999628067016602, -1.1323045834288337e-09, 0.00862560048699379)
            }

            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("GeneralAbility"):FireServer(unpack(args))
            task.wait(1)

            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Success",
                Content = "Tycoon placed at safe spot!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Tycoon Glove",
                Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "🗿",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false

    Name = "1-2-3 Quest"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura
local moaiToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        moaiToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while moaiToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralAbility with CFrame (every 14 seconds)
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                            if safespot then
                                local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                if base then
                                    local args = {
                                        [1] = base.CFrame
                                    }
                                    generalAbility:FireServer(unpack(args))
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(14)
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "🗿",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then return end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Obby",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false

    Name = "1-2-3 Quest (SOON REWORK)"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1 Quest"
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Obby Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        task.spawn(function()
            local players = game:GetService("Players")
            local replicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local localPlayer = players.LocalPlayer

            while true do
                pcall(function()
                    for _, player in ipairs(players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if player ~= localPlayer then
                            local character = player.Character
                            if character then
                                local leftArm = character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")
                                if leftArm then
                                    replicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(leftArm)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end
})

-- ===== VOODOO TAB =====
end
do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Voodoo",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quest (SOON REWORK)"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2 Quest"
})

local voodooRunning = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Slap Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(AutoSlapVoodoo)
        voodooRunning = AutoSlapVoodoo
        if not voodooRunning then return end

        task.spawn(function()
            local Players = game:GetService("Players")
            local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
            local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

            local function teleportToRandomPlayer()
                local playerList = Players:GetPlayers()
                if #playerList > 1 then
                    local randomPlayer = nil
                    repeat
                        randomPlayer = playerList[math.random(1, #playerList)]
                    until randomPlayer ~= LocalPlayer

                    local targetChar = randomPlayer.Character
                    if targetChar and targetChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                        local hrp = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if hrp then
                            hrp.CFrame = targetChar.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            local function fireGeneralHitForAllPlayers()
                for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player ~= LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                        local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or 
                                          player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or
                                          player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
                        if targetPart then
                            ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                        end
                    end
                end
            end

            local count = 0
            while voodooRunning and count < 750 do
                if LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Voodoo" then
                    teleportToRandomPlayer()
                    fireGeneralHitForAllPlayers()
                    count = count + 1
                    task.wait(0.5)
                else
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Error",
                        Content = "Equip Voodoo Glove",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                    break
                end
            end
        end)
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "3 Quest"
})

local voodooAbilityToggle = false
local voodooAbilityLoop = nil

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Voodoo Spam Ability Without CD",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(state)
        voodooAbilityToggle = state
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        if voodooAbilityToggle then
            if player.leaderstats and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Voodoo" then
                voodooAbilityLoop = task.spawn(function()
                    while voodooAbilityToggle and player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Voodoo" do
                        game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").GeneralAbility:FireServer()
                        task.wait(3.5)
                    end
                end)
            else
                voodooAbilityToggle = false
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Voodoo Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
            end
        else
            if voodooAbilityLoop then
                task.cancel(voodooAbilityLoop)
                voodooAbilityLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

-- ===== ROB TAB =====
end
do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "rob",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({

Section = Tab:AddSection({

})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1 Quest"
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Create Null Portal (Need Bob And Rob Gloves)",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local hrp = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        
        if not hrp then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Character not found!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new()
        task.wait(0.5)

        local robClick = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("rob") and workspace.Lobby.rob:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
        if robClick then
            fireclickdetector(robClick)
        end
        task.wait(0.5)
        
        local robRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("rob")
        if robRemote then
            robRemote:FireServer()
        end
        task.wait(0.5)

        local bobClick = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby") and workspace.Lobby:FindFirstChild("bob") and workspace.Lobby.bob:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
        if bobClick then
            fireclickdetector(bobClick)
        end
        task.wait(0.5)
        
        local bobRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("bob")
        if bobRemote then
            bobRemote:FireServer()
        end

        OrionLib:MakeNotification({
            Name = "Done",
            Content = "Null Portal sequence completed!",
            Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
            Time = 3
        })
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "2 Quest"
})

local Walkspeed = 20
local KeepWalkspeed = false

Tab:AddSlider({
    Name = "WalkSpeed",
    Min = 20,
    Max = 1000,
    Default = 20,
    Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
    Increment = 1,
    ValueName = "WalkSpeed",
    Callback = function(Value)
        Walkspeed = Value
        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if char then
            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
            if humanoid then
                humanoid.WalkSpeed = Value
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "WalkSpeed",
    Default = "20",
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        local num = tonumber(Value)
        if num then
            Walkspeed = num
            local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if char then
                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                if humanoid then
                    humanoid.WalkSpeed = num
                end
            end
        end
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Walkspeed Set Auto",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        KeepWalkspeed = Value
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while KeepWalkspeed do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                            if humanoid and humanoid.WalkSpeed ~= Walkspeed then
                                humanoid.WalkSpeed = Walkspeed
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait()
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "3 Quest"
})

local AutoAbsorb = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Absorb People",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoAbsorb = Value
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

        if AutoAbsorb then
            if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value:lower() == "rob" then
                task.spawn(function()
                    while AutoAbsorb do
                        pcall(function()
                            local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
                            local target = nil
                            local attempts = 0
                            
                            while not target and attempts < 20 do
                                attempts = attempts + 1
                                local randomPlayer = players[math.random(1, #players)]
                                if randomPlayer ~= player and randomPlayer.Character and randomPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
                                    target = randomPlayer
                                end
                            end

                            if target then
                                local targetHRP = target.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                local playerHRP = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                
                                if targetHRP and playerHRP then
                                    playerHRP.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 0, 2)
                                end

                                local ability = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Ability")
                                if ability then
                                    ability:FireServer()
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        task.wait(1)
                    end
                end)
            else
                AutoAbsorb = false
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Rob Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
            end
        end
    end
})

local autoRobLoop = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Rob Transformation",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoRobLoop = Value
        
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while autoRobLoop do
                    pcall(function()
                        local robObject = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby")
                        if robObject then
                            robObject = robObject:FindFirstChild("rob")
                            if robObject and robObject:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
                                fireclickdetector(robObject.ClickDetector)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local robRemote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("rob")
                        if robRemote then
                            robRemote:FireServer()
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(17)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura
local tinkererToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        tinkererToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while tinkererToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralAbility (every 7 seconds)
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(7)
                        
                        -- TinkererHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local tinkererHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("TinkererHit")
                        if tinkererHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        tinkererHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Tinkerer",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then return end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

end
do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Firework",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quest"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Slap Aura + Ability + Firework + Jump
local autoReceiver = false
local receiverLoop = nil
local slapAuraConnection = nil
local abilityConnection = nil
local fireworkConnection = nil
local jumpTimer = 0
local abilityTimer = 0
local slapTimer = 0
local fireworkTimer = 0

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Receiver (Safespot + Ability + Firework + Jump + Slap Aura)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoReceiver = Value
        
        if Value then
            -- Reset timers
            jumpTimer = 0
            abilityTimer = 0
            slapTimer = 0
            fireworkTimer = 0
            
            -- Start main loop for Safespot (every 0.01 seconds) and Jump (every 3 seconds)
            if receiverLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverLoop)
                receiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            receiverLoop = task.spawn(function()
                local jumpTimer = 0
                
                while autoReceiver do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then return end
                        
                        -- 1. Teleport to Safespot (every 0.01 seconds)
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base and base:IsA("BasePart") then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- 2. Auto jump every 4 seconds
                        jumpTimer = jumpTimer + 0.01
                        if jumpTimer >= 4 then
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                            if humanoid then
                                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
                            end
                            jumpTimer = 0
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.01) -- Safespot teleport every 0.01 seconds
                end
            end)
            
            -- Start Auto Teleport to Firework (every 1 second)
            if fireworkConnection then
                fireworkConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkConnection = nil
            end
            
            fireworkConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                if not autoReceiver then 
                    fireworkConnection:Disconnect()
                    fireworkConnection = nil
                    return 
                end
                
                fireworkTimer = fireworkTimer + deltaTime
                if fireworkTimer >= 1 then
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then return end
                        
                        local playerName = player.Name
                        local fireworkPart = workspace:FindFirstChild("Firework_" .. playerName)
                        if fireworkPart and fireworkPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                            hrp.CFrame = fireworkPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
                        end
                    end)
                    fireworkTimer = 0
                end
            end)
            
            -- Start Auto Use Ability (every 3 seconds)
            if abilityConnection then
                abilityConnection:Disconnect()
                abilityConnection = nil
            end
            
            abilityConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                if not autoReceiver then 
                    abilityConnection:Disconnect()
                    abilityConnection = nil
                    return 
                end
                
                abilityTimer = abilityTimer + deltaTime
                if abilityTimer >= 3 then
                    pcall(function()
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                    end)
                    abilityTimer = 0
                end
            end)
            
            -- Start Slap Aura (every 3 seconds)
            if slapAuraConnection then
                slapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                slapAuraConnection = nil
            end
            
            slapAuraConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(deltaTime)
                if not autoReceiver then 
                    slapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnection = nil
                    return 
                end
                
                slapTimer = slapTimer + deltaTime
                if slapTimer >= 3 then
                    pcall(function()
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if not generalHit then return end
                        
                        for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                            if player ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                                local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm") or 
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm") or
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or 
                                                  player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if targetPart then
                                    generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    slapTimer = 0
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Receiver",
                Content = "Enabled! Safespot at 0.01s, Firework at 1s, others at 3s.",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            -- Stop main loop
            if receiverLoop then
                task.cancel(receiverLoop)
                receiverLoop = nil
            end
            
            -- Stop Firework
            if fireworkConnection then
                fireworkConnection:Disconnect()
                fireworkConnection = nil
            end
            
            -- Stop Ability
            if abilityConnection then
                abilityConnection:Disconnect()
                abilityConnection = nil
            end
            
            -- Stop Slap Aura
            if slapAuraConnection then
                slapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                slapAuraConnection = nil
            end
            
            jumpTimer = 0
            abilityTimer = 0
            slapTimer = 0
            fireworkTimer = 0
            
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Helper"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Die on Ragdoll + Firework + Jump
local autoHelper = false
local helperLoop = nil
local helperJumpTimer = 0

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Helper (Safespot + Firework + Jump + Die on Ragdoll + Auto Re-enter)",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoHelper = Value
        
        if Value then
            helperJumpTimer = 0
            
            if helperLoop then
                task.cancel(helperLoop)
                helperLoop = nil
            end
            
            helperLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while autoHelper do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        if not char then 
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return 
                        end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if not hrp then 
                            task.wait(0.5)
                            return 
                        end
                        
                        -- 1. Teleport to Safespot (Receiver position)
                        hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        
                        -- 2. Auto teleport to Firework (any basepart with "Firework" in name)
                        for _, part in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
                            if part:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(part.Name, "Firework") then
                                hrp.CFrame = part.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)
                                break
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- 3. Auto jump every 4 seconds
                        helperJumpTimer = helperJumpTimer + 0.5
                        if helperJumpTimer >= 4 then
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                            if humanoid then
                                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
                            end
                            helperJumpTimer = 0
                        end
                        
                        -- 4. Check if entered exists
                        local entered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        
                        if entered == nil then
                            -- If entered doesn't exist, teleport to arena position
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        else
                            -- 5. If entered exists, check for Ragdolled
                            local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                            if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                                -- Die on ragdoll
                                local humanoid = char:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                                if humanoid then
                                    humanoid.Health = 0
                                    task.wait(2) -- Wait for respawn
                                    
                                    -- Auto re-enter arena after respawn
                                    local newChar = player.Character
                                    if newChar then
                                        local newHrp = newChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                        if newHrp then
                                            newHrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                                            task.wait(0.5)
                                        end
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Auto Helper",
                Content = "Enabled! Teleporting to Safespot, Firework, Jumping & monitoring ragdoll.",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            
        else
            if helperLoop then
                task.cancel(helperLoop)
                helperLoop = nil
            end
            
            helperJumpTimer = 0
            
        end
    end
})

end

do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Run",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quests (SOON REWORK)"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2 Quests"
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Closest Player",
    Callback = function()
        local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
        local localChar = LocalPlayer.Character
        local localHRP = localChar and localChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        
        if not localHRP then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Your character not found!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                Time = 2
            })
            return
        end
        
        local closestPlayer = nil
        local closestDistance = math.huge
        local closestPos = nil
        
        for _, player in ipairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
            if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                local character = player.Character
                local hrp = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if hrp then
                    local distance = (hrp.Position - localHRP.Position).Magnitude
                    if distance < closestDistance then
                        closestDistance = distance
                        closestPlayer = player
                        closestPos = hrp.Position
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        if closestPlayer and closestPos then
            localHRP.CFrame = CFrame.new(closestPos)
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Teleported",
                Content = "Teleported to " .. closestPlayer.Name .. " (" .. math.floor(closestDistance) .. " studs away)",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 2
            })
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "No other players found!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                Time = 2
            })
        end
    end
})

local positionValue = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
local secondsValue = 7

local positionInput = Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "Put Position (x, y, z)",
    Default = "0, 0, 0",
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        local parts = {}
        for part in string.gmatch(Value, "([^,]+)") do
            table.insert(parts, tonumber(part))
        end
        
        if #parts >= 3 and parts[1] and parts[2] and parts[3] then
            positionValue = Vector3.new(parts[1], parts[2], parts[3])
        else
            positionValue = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        end
    end
})

local secondsInput = Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "Repeat Ability Seconds Delay",
    Default = "7",
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        local num = tonumber(Value)
        if num and num > 0 then
            secondsValue = num
        else
            secondsValue = 7
        end
    end
})

local autoRunEnabled = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Use Run Ability",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoRunEnabled = Value
        
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while autoRunEnabled do
                    pcall(function()
                        local args = {
                            [1] = positionValue
                        }
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(secondsValue)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

do
local Tab = Window:MakeTab({
    Name = "Frostbite",
    Icon = "rbxassetid://7734068321",
    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3-4 Quests"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "Receiver"
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura
local frostbiteToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        frostbiteToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while frostbiteToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralAbility with float (every 4 seconds)
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer(0.012500000651925802)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(4)
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Frostbite",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end

    Name = "Helper"

-- Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Receiver + Auto Die On Ragdoll",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while Value do
                    pcall(function()
                        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local char = player.Character
                        
                        if not char or not char.Parent then
                            char = player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                            task.wait(1)
                        end
                        
                        if not char then return end
                        
                        local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                        
                        if not hrp or not humanoid then return end
                        
                        local hasEntered = char:FindFirstChild("entered")
                        if not hasEntered then
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(-1209, 328, 3)
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                        
                        local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                        if safespot then
                            local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                            if base then
                                hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(10000, -42, 9996)
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        
                        local ragdolled = char:FindFirstChild("Ragdolled")
                        if ragdolled and ragdolled.Value == true then
                            humanoid.Health = 0
                            task.wait(0.5)
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

    Name = "Plank",

    PremiumOnly = false
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quests (SOON REWORK)"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "|||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||||"
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "1-2-3 Quests"
})

_G.AutoPlank = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Use Plank On Players",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        _G.AutoPlank = Value
        
        if Value then
            task.spawn(function()
                while _G.AutoPlank do
                    pcall(function()
                        local players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
                        local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                        local targetPlayers = {}
                        
                        for _, player in ipairs(players) do
                            if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                local hrp = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if hrp then
                                    table.insert(targetPlayers, {
                                        player = player,
                                        position = hrp.Position
                                    })
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        if #targetPlayers > 0 then
                            local randomTarget = targetPlayers[math.random(1, #targetPlayers)]
                            
                            local args = {
                                [1] = "OutOfBody",
                                [2] = {
                                    ["mousebehavior"] = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default,
                                    ["ismoving"] = false,
                                    ["dir"] = Vector3.new(
                                        randomTarget.position.X,
                                        randomTarget.position.Y,
                                        randomTarget.position.Z
                                    )
                                }
                            }
                            
                            local blink = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("Blink")
                            if blink then
                                blink:FireServer(unpack(args))
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.1)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

-- Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura
local hexaToggle = false

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Teleport To Safespot + Auto Use Ability + Slap Aura",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        hexaToggle = Value
        
        if Value then
            local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
            if not safespot then
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Safespot not found! Create Safespot first.",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                    Time = 3
                })
                return false
            end
            
            task.spawn(function()
                while hexaToggle do
                    pcall(function()
                        local char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                        if char then
                            local hrp = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                            if hrp then
                                local safespot = workspace:FindFirstChild("Safespot")
                                if safespot then
                                    local base = safespot:FindFirstChild("Base")
                                    if base then
                                        hrp.CFrame = base.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 10, 0)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                        
                        -- GeneralAbility (every 10 seconds)
                        local generalAbility = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralAbility")
                        if generalAbility then
                            generalAbility:FireServer()
                        end
                        
                        task.wait(10)
                        
                        -- GeneralHit Slap Aura (every 0.5 seconds)
                        local generalHit = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("GeneralHit")
                        if generalHit then
                            local localPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                            for _, player in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
                                if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                                    local targetPart = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or 
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or
                                                      player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                    if targetPart then
                                        generalHit:FireServer(targetPart)
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Hexa",
                Content = "Auto Teleport + Ability + Slap Aura Enabled!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end

local carKeysToggle = false
local upgradeLoop = nil

local attributeFrames = {
    "UtilityAttributeFrame",
    "ArmorAttributeFrame",
    "ReverseAttributeFrame",
    "SteerAngleAttributeFrame",
    "AccelerationAttributeFrame",
    "MaxSpeedAttributeFrame",
    "KnockbackAttributeFrame"
}

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Upgrade All Stats",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        carKeysToggle = Value
        if carKeysToggle then
            upgradeLoop = task.spawn(function()
                while carKeysToggle do
                    for _, attr in ipairs(attributeFrames) do
                        local args = { attr }
                        local carKeysUpgrade = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("CarKeysUpgrade")
                        if carKeysUpgrade then
                            carKeysUpgrade:FireServer(unpack(args))
                        end
                        task.wait(0.1)
                    end
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        else
            if upgradeLoop then
                task.cancel(upgradeLoop)
                upgradeLoop = nil
            end
        end
    end
})

Section = Tab:AddSection({
    Name = "2-3 Quest"
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Car Keys Slap Aura",
    Callback = function()
        local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
        if player.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Car Keys" then
            task.spawn(function()
                local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
                local Players = game:GetService("Players")
                local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

                while true do
                    pcall(function()
                        for _, player in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                            if player ~= LocalPlayer and player.Character then
                                local rightArm = player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm")
                                if rightArm then
                                    ReplicatedStorage.GeneralHit:FireServer(rightArm)
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    task.wait(0.5)
                end
            end)
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Equip Car Keys",
                Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})
