-- Store owned badges
local ownedBadges = {}

-- Fetch owned badges from ReplicatedStorage
local function fetchOwnedBadges()
    ownedBadges = {}
    
    local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
    if not playerData then
        return false
    end
    
    local playerFolder = playerData:FindFirstChild(username)
    if not playerFolder then
        return false
    end
    
    local unlockedBadges = playerFolder:FindFirstChild("UnlockedBadges")
    if not unlockedBadges then
        return false
    end
    
    if unlockedBadges:IsA("StringValue") then
        local badgeIdsString = unlockedBadges.Value
        
        if badgeIdsString and badgeIdsString ~= "" then
            local trimmed = badgeIdsString:sub(2, -2)
            
            for id in string.gmatch(trimmed, "[^,]+") do
                local cleanId = id:match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
                ownedBadges[cleanId] = true
            end
        end
        return true
    end
    return false
end

local WebhookSettings = {
    WebhookURL = "",
    SendInterval = "No time",
    LoggedObjects = {},
    SlapsThreshold = 0,
    NullShardsThreshold = 0,
    Enabled = false,
    PingType = "No Pings",
    UserID = "",
    RoleID = "",
    
    -- Tracking variables
    LastSlapsValue = 0,
    LastNullShardsValue = 0,
    TrackedSlaps = false,
    TrackedNullShards = false,
    SlapsStartValue = 0,
    NullShardsStartValue = 0,
    IsSlapsTracking = false,
    IsNullShardsTracking = false,
    ObjectLogged = {},
    SlapsLogged = false,
    NullShardsLogged = false,
    SlappleLogged = {},
    GoldenSlappleLogged = false,
    LastBadgeCheck = {},
    BadgeLogSent = false,
}

-- ============================================================
-- HELPER FUNCTIONS
-- ============================================================

-- Helper function to get Null Shards
function WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
    local playerData = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("PlayerData")
    if playerData then
        local userData = playerData:FindFirstChild(username)
        if userData then
            local nullShards = userData:FindFirstChild("NullShards")
            if nullShards then
                return nullShards.Value
            end
        end
    end
    return 0
end

-- Get ping prefix based on settings
local function getPingPrefix()
    if WebhookSettings.PingType == "No Pings" then
        return ""
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@User Ping" and WebhookSettings.UserID ~= "" then
        return "<@" .. WebhookSettings.UserID .. "> "
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Role Ping" and WebhookSettings.RoleID ~= "" then
        return "<@&" .. WebhookSettings.RoleID .. "> "
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Everyone Ping" then
        return "@everyone "
    elseif WebhookSettings.PingType == "@Here Ping" then
        return "@here "
    end
    return ""
end

-- Webhook send function
local function sendWebhookMessage(content)
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.WebhookURL == "" then return end
    
    local ping = getPingPrefix()
    local fullContent = ping .. content
    
    local payload = {
        content = fullContent or "No message provided"
    }
    
    local jsonData = HttpService:JSONEncode(payload)
    
    local success, response = pcall(function()
        if syn and syn.request then
            return syn.request({
                Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                Method = "POST",
                Headers = {
                    ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                },
                Body = jsonData
            })
        elseif http_request then
            return http_request({
                Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                Method = "POST",
                Headers = {
                    ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                },
                Body = jsonData
            })
        elseif request then
            return request({
                Url = WebhookSettings.WebhookURL,
                Method = "POST",
                Headers = {
                    ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                },
                Body = jsonData
            })
        else
            warn("No request method available for webhook!")
            return nil, "No request method available"
        end
    end)
    
    if not success then
        warn("Failed to send webhook: " .. tostring(response))
    end
end

-- Get badge name from ID
local function getBadgeName(badgeId)
    for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
        if badge.id == badgeId then
            return badge.name
        end
    end
    return "Unknown Badge"
end

-- ============================================================
-- UI ELEMENTS
-- ============================================================

-- 1. Webhook URL Textbox
local WebhookTextbox = Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "Webhook URL",
    Default = "",
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        WebhookSettings.WebhookURL = Value
    end
})

-- 2. Send Interval Dropdown
local IntervalDropdown = Tab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Send Interval",
    Options = {"No time", "30 Seconds", "1 Minute", "10 Minutes", "30 Minutes", "1 Hour", "5 Hours", "10 Hours", "1 Day"},
    Default = "No time",
    Callback = function(Value)
        WebhookSettings.SendInterval = Value
    end,
    Flag = "webhookInterval",
    Save = true
})

-- 3. Multi Dropdown for Objects
local ObjectsMultiDropdown = Tab:AddMultiDropdown({
    Name = "Choose Objects Spawns To Log",
    Options = {"Jet Orb", "Phase Orb", "Glitch Orb", "Siphon Orb", "MATERIALIZE Orb", "Slapple", "Golden Slapple", "Toolbox"},
    Default = {},
    Callback = function(Values)
        WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects = Values
        WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged = {}
        WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged = {}
        WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
        for _, obj in pairs(Values) do
            if obj == "Slapple" then
                WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[obj] = {}
            elseif obj == "Golden Slapple" then
                WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
            else
                WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[obj] = false
            end
        end
    end,
    Flag = "loggedObjects",
    Save = true
})

-- 4. Slaps Threshold Dropdown
local SlapsDropdown = Tab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Slaps Threshold",
    Options = {"100+ Slaps", "1000+ Slaps", "10000+ Slaps", "100000+ Slaps", "1000000+ Slaps", "Custom Slaps Amount"},
    Default = "1000+ Slaps",
    Callback = function(Value)
        if Value == "Custom Slaps Amount" then
            WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold = 0
        else
            local num = tonumber(Value:match("(%d+)")) or 0
            WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold = num
            WebhookSettings.TrackedSlaps = false
            WebhookSettings.SlapsLogged = false
        end
    end,
    Flag = "slapsThreshold",
    Save = true
})

-- 7. Enable/Disable Toggle
local EnableToggle = Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Enable Webhook Logging",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(value)
        if value then
            WebhookSettings.Enabled = true
            
            -- Initialize tracking
            WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue = LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value
            WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue = WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
            WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue = WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue
            WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue = WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue
            WebhookSettings.IsSlapsTracking = true
            WebhookSettings.IsNullShardsTracking = true
            WebhookSettings.SlapsLogged = false
            WebhookSettings.NullShardsLogged = false
            WebhookSettings.BadgeLogSent = false
            WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged = {}
            WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged = {}
            WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
            WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck = {}
            
            -- Fetch initial badges
            pcall(fetchOwnedBadges)
            for badgeId, _ in pairs(ownedBadges) do
                WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] = true
            end
            
            for _, obj in pairs(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects) do
                if obj == "Slapple" then
                    WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[obj] = {}
                elseif obj == "Golden Slapple" then
                    WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                else
                    WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[obj] = false
                end
            end
            sendWebhookMessage("✅ Webhook logging **STARTED**!")
        else
            -- Send stop message before disabling
            sendWebhookMessage("🛑 Webhook logging **STOPPED**!")
            WebhookSettings.Enabled = false
        end
    end
})

-- ============================================================
-- TRACKING FUNCTIONS
-- ============================================================

-- Object detection function
local function checkObjectSpawns()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled then return end
    
    -- Regular objects (not Slapples)
    local objectsToCheck = {
        ["Jet Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("JetOrb"),
        ["Phase Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("PhaseOrb"),
        ["Glitch Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("GlitchOrb"),
        ["Siphon Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("SiphonOrb"),
        ["MATERIALIZE Orb"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("MATERIALIZEOrb"),
        ["Toolbox"] = workspace:FindFirstChild("Toolbox"),
    }
    
    for name, object in pairs(objectsToCheck) do
        if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, name) then
            if object and not WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] then
                WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] = true
                
                local placeName = "Unknown"
                pcall(function()
                    local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                    if info and info.Name then
                        placeName = info.Name
                    end
                end)
                
                local message = string.format(
                    "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** %s\n\n**Name:** %s\n**Real Name:** %s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                    name, name, object.Name, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                )
                
                sendWebhookMessage(message)
            elseif not object then
                WebhookSettings.ObjectLogged[name] = false
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- SLAPPLE CHECK (workspace.Arena.island5.Slapples)
    if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, "Slapple") then
        local slapplesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
        if slapplesFolder then
            local island5 = slapplesFolder:FindFirstChild("island5")
            if island5 then
                local slapples = island5:FindFirstChild("Slapples")
                if slapples then
                    for _, model in ipairs(slapples:GetChildren()) do
                        if model:IsA("Model") then
                            local gloveMesh = model:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                            if gloveMesh and gloveMesh:IsA("MeshPart") then
                                local transparency = gloveMesh.Transparency
                                local modelName = model.Name
                                
                                if not WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] then
                                    if transparency == 0 then
                                        WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] = true
                                        
                                        local placeName = "Unknown"
                                        pcall(function()
                                            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                                            if info and info.Name then
                                                placeName = info.Name
                                            end
                                        end)
                                        
                                        local message = string.format(
                                            "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** Slapple\n\n**Name:** Slapple\n**Real Name:** %s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                                            modelName, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                                        )
                                        
                                        sendWebhookMessage(message)
                                    end
                                elseif transparency == 1 then
                                    WebhookSettings.SlappleLogged[modelName] = nil
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- GOLDEN SLAPPLE CHECK
    if table.find(WebhookSettings.LoggedObjects, "Golden Slapple") then
        local slapplesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Arena")
        if slapplesFolder then
            local island5 = slapplesFolder:FindFirstChild("island5")
            if island5 then
                local slapples = island5:FindFirstChild("Slapples")
                if slapples then
                    local goldenSlapple = slapples:FindFirstChild("GoldenSlapple")
                    if goldenSlapple and goldenSlapple:IsA("Model") then
                        local gloveMesh = goldenSlapple:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                        if gloveMesh and gloveMesh:IsA("MeshPart") then
                            local transparency = gloveMesh.Transparency
                            
                            if transparency == 0 and not WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged then
                                WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = true
                                
                                local placeName = "Unknown"
                                pcall(function()
                                    local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
                                    if info and info.Name then
                                        placeName = info.Name
                                    end
                                end)
                                
                                local message = string.format(
                                    "**From Webhook Log:**\n\n**Detected | Spawned:** Golden Slapple\n\n**Name:** Golden Slapple\n**Real Name:** GoldenSlapple\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
                                    placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
                                )
                                
                                sendWebhookMessage(message)
                            elseif transparency == 1 then
                                WebhookSettings.GoldenSlappleLogged = false
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Slaps tracking function
local function checkSlaps()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold == 0 or not WebhookSettings.IsSlapsTracking then return end
    
    local currentSlaps = LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Slaps.Value
    local previousSlaps = WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue
    
    if currentSlaps >= WebhookSettings.SlapsThreshold and currentSlaps > previousSlaps then
        WebhookSettings.LastSlapsValue = currentSlaps
        
        local earnedSlaps = currentSlaps - WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue
        
        local placeName = "Unknown"
        pcall(function()
            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
            if info and info.Name then
                placeName = info.Name
            end
        end)
        
        local message = string.format(
            "**Slaps Counter Log**\n\n**Name:** Slaps\n**Before Amount:** %s\n**After Amount:** %s\n**Earned Total Slaps:** +%s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
            WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue, currentSlaps, earnedSlaps, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
        )
        
        sendWebhookMessage(message)
        
        WebhookSettings.SlapsStartValue = currentSlaps
    end
end

-- Null Shards tracking function
local function checkNullShards()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled or WebhookSettings.NullShardsThreshold == 0 or not WebhookSettings.IsNullShardsTracking then return end
    
    local currentNullShards = WebhookSettings:GetNullShards()
    local previousNullShards = WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue
    
    if currentNullShards >= WebhookSettings.NullShardsThreshold and currentNullShards > previousNullShards then
        WebhookSettings.LastNullShardsValue = currentNullShards
        
        local earnedNullShards = currentNullShards - WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue
        
        local placeName = "Unknown"
        pcall(function()
            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
            if info and info.Name then
                placeName = info.Name
            end
        end)
        
        local message = string.format(
            "**Null Shards Counter Log**\n\n**Name:** Null Shards\n**Before Amount:** %s\n**After Amount:** %s\n**Earned Total Null Shards:** +%s\n**Place Name:** %s\n**Place ID:** %s\n**JobID:** %s",
            WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue, currentNullShards, earnedNullShards, placeName, game.PlaceId, game.JobId
        )
        
        sendWebhookMessage(message)
        
        WebhookSettings.NullShardsStartValue = currentNullShards
    end
end

-- Badge tracking function
local function checkBadges()
    if not WebhookSettings.Enabled then return end
    
    -- Fetch latest badges
    local success = pcall(fetchOwnedBadges)
    if not success then return end
    
    local newBadges = {}
    
    -- Check for new badges
    for badgeId, _ in pairs(ownedBadges) do
        if not WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] then
            table.insert(newBadges, badgeId)
            WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck[badgeId] = true
        end
    end
    
    -- If there are new badges, send a log
    if #newBadges > 0 then
        local placeName = "Unknown"
        pcall(function()
            local info = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(game.PlaceId)
            if info and info.Name then
                placeName = info.Name
            end
        end)
        
        -- Find badge names
        local newBadgeNames = {}
        for _, id in pairs(newBadges) do
            for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
                if badge.id == id then
                    table.insert(newBadgeNames, badge.name .. " (`" .. id .. "`)")
                    break
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Build owned list (all badges)
        local ownedList = {}
        for id, _ in pairs(WebhookSettings.LastBadgeCheck) do
            table.insert(ownedList, id)
        end
        
        -- Build missing list (all glove-rewarding badges not owned)
        local missingList = {}
        for _, badge in pairs(allBadges) do
            if badge.category == "GloveRewarding" and not ownedBadges[badge.id] then
                table.insert(missingList, badge.id)
            end
        end
        
        local message = string.format(
            "**🎉 NEW BADGE(S) UNLOCKED!**\n\n" ..
            "**Badge(s):**\n%s\n\n" ..
            "**Place Name:** %s\n" ..
            "**Place ID:** %s\n" ..
            "**JobID:** %s\n\n" ..
            "**Total Badges Unlocked:** %s\n" ..
            "**Missing Glove Badges:** %s",
            table.concat(newBadgeNames, "\n"),
            placeName,
            game.PlaceId,
            game.JobId,
            #ownedList > 0 and #ownedList .. " badges" or "None",
            #missingList > 0 and #missingList .. " badges" or "None"
        )
        
        sendWebhookMessage(message)
    end
end

-- Main loop
local function startWebhookLoop()
    while true do
        if WebhookSettings.Enabled then
            pcall(checkObjectSpawns)
            pcall(checkSlaps)
            pcall(checkNullShards)
            pcall(checkBadges)
        end
        
        local waitTime = 1
        if WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "30 Seconds" then 
            waitTime = 30
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Minute" then 
            waitTime = 60
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "10 Minutes" then 
            waitTime = 600
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "30 Minutes" then 
            waitTime = 1800
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Hour" then 
            waitTime = 3600
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "5 Hours" then 
            waitTime = 18000
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "10 Hours" then 
            waitTime = 36000
        elseif WebhookSettings.SendInterval == "1 Day" then 
            waitTime = 86400
        end
        
        task.wait(waitTime)
    end
end

-- Start the loop
task.spawn(startWebhookLoop)

end

-- Variables
local deathSoundEnabled = false
local currentSoundId = ""
local monitorConnection = nil
local childAddedConnections = {}

-- Function to clean up old connections
local function cleanupConnections()
    if monitorConnection then
        monitorConnection:Disconnect()
        monitorConnection = nil
    end
    
    for _, conn in pairs(childAddedConnections) do
        pcall(function()
            conn:Disconnect()
        end)
    end
    childAddedConnections = {}
end

-- Function to modify death sounds in a character
local function modifyDeathSounds(character)
    if not deathSoundEnabled then return end
    if not character then return end
    
    local torso = character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
    if not torso then return end
    
    for _, sound in pairs(torso:GetChildren()) do
        if sound:IsA("Sound") then
            local soundName = sound.Name:lower()
            if soundName:find("death") or soundName:find("die") then
                pcall(function()
                    if sound.SoundId ~= currentSoundId then
                        sound.SoundId = currentSoundId
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Function to setup listener for new sounds
local function setupSoundListener(character)
    if not character then return end
    
    local torso = character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
    if not torso then return end
    
    local connection = torso.ChildAdded:Connect(function(child)
        if child:IsA("Sound") and deathSoundEnabled then
            local soundName = child.Name:lower()
            if soundName:find("death") or soundName:find("die") then
                task.wait(0.1)
                pcall(function()
                    child.SoundId = currentSoundId
                end)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    table.insert(childAddedConnections, connection)
end

-- Function to start monitoring
local function startMonitoring()
    if monitorConnection then return end
    
    monitorConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        if deathSoundEnabled then
            local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            if character then
                modifyDeathSounds(character)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    -- Setup listener for current character
    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    if character then
        setupSoundListener(character)
    end
end

-- Function to stop monitoring
local function stopMonitoring()
    cleanupConnections()
end

-- Function to update all existing death sounds
local function updateAllDeathSounds()
    if not deathSoundEnabled then return end
    
    local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
    if character then
        local torso = character:FindFirstChild("Torso") or character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
        if torso then
            for _, sound in pairs(torso:GetChildren()) do
                if sound:IsA("Sound") then
                    local soundName = sound.Name:lower()
                    if soundName:find("death") or soundName:find("die") then
                        pcall(function()
                            sound.SoundId = currentSoundId
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Add Sound ID TextBox
Tab:AddParagraph("Custom Sound ID:", "Enter your sound ID below (format: rbxassetid://1234567890)")

local soundIdBox = Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "Put Custom Sound ID",
    Default = currentSoundId,
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(value)
        if value and value ~= "" then
            -- Ensure it has rbxassetid:// prefix if not present
            if not value:find("rbxassetid://") then
                currentSoundId = "rbxassetid://" .. value
            else
                currentSoundId = value
            end
            
            -- Update existing sounds if enabled
            if deathSoundEnabled then
                updateAllDeathSounds()
            end
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Sound ID Updated",
                Content = "New sound ID: " .. currentSoundId,
                Time = 2
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Add Toggle for auto apply
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Apply Death Sound",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(value)
        deathSoundEnabled = value
        
        if value then
            startMonitoring()
            updateAllDeathSounds()
            
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Death Sound Modifier",
                Content = "Enabled! Death sounds will be changed to: " .. currentSoundId,
                Time = 3
            })
        else
            stopMonitoring()
            
        end
    end
})

-- Handle character respawn
game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
    task.wait(0.5)
    
    if deathSoundEnabled then
        setupSoundListener(character)
        task.wait(0.2)
        modifyDeathSounds(character)
    end
end)

-- Initial setup
startMonitoring()

-- Variables
local nametagText = ""
local autoNametag = false
local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer

-- Textbox for nametag
Tab:AddTextbox({
    Name = "Type Ur Own Any Nametag",
    Default = "",
    TextDisappear = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        nametagText = Value
    end
})

-- Button to apply nametag once
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Change Nametag",
    Callback = function()
        if nametagText == "" then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Please enter text in the textbox first!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
            return
        end
        
        -- Find and update nametag
        local character = player.Character
        if character then
            local nametag = character:FindFirstChild("Head") and character.Head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
            if nametag then
                local topLabel = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels") and nametag.Labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
                if topLabel then
                    topLabel.Text = nametagText
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Success",
                        Content = "Nametag changed to: " .. nametagText,
                        Image = "rbxassetid://4483345998",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                else
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Error",
                        Content = "TopLabel not found!",
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                end
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Nametag not found!",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
            end
        else
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Error",
                Content = "Character not found!",
                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 3
            })
        end
    end
})

-- Toggle for auto nametag
Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Change Nametag",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        autoNametag = Value
        if Value then
            -- Start auto nametag loop
            task.spawn(function()
                while autoNametag do
                    if nametagText ~= "" then
                        local character = player.Character
                        if character then
                            local nametag = character:FindFirstChild("Head") and character.Head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
                            if nametag then
                                local topLabel = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels") and nametag.Labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
                                if topLabel then
                                    topLabel.Text = nametagText
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    task.wait(0.01)
                end
            end)
        end
    end
})

-- Auto reapply nametag when character respawns
player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
    if autoNametag and nametagText ~= "" then
        -- Wait for character to fully load
        wait(2)
        local nametag = character:FindFirstChild("Head") and character.Head:FindFirstChild("Nametag")
        if nametag then
            local topLabel = nametag:FindFirstChild("Labels") and nametag.Labels:FindFirstChild("TopLabel")
            if topLabel then
                topLabel.Text = nametagText
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ==========================================
-- BACKPACK V2 TOGGLE
-- ==========================================

_G.BackpackV2 = false
_G.BackpackV2Loop = true
_G.ConnectFun = _G.ConnectFun or {}

-- Store original positions
if _G.Backpack == nil then
    _G.Backpack = {
        ["Old"] = {
            ["Hotbar"] = game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar.Position,
            ["Inventory"] = game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory.Position,
            ["Backpack Number"] = {}
        },
        ["New"] = {
            ["Hotbar"] = (game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar.Position + UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -10)),
            ["Inventory"] = (game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory.Position + UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -10)),
            ["Backpack Number"] = {}
        }
    }
    wait()
    for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:GetChildren()) do
        if v:IsA("TextButton") then
            _G.Backpack["Old"]["Backpack Number"][v.Name] = v.Position
            _G.Backpack["New"]["Backpack Number"][v.Name] = UDim2.new(0, 3, 0, 3)
        end
    end
end

-- Main loop for backpack styling
spawn(function()
    while _G.BackpackV2Loop do
        if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Hotbar") then
            game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar.Position = (_G.BackpackV2 == true and (_G.Backpack["New"]["Hotbar"]) or (_G.Backpack["Old"]["Hotbar"]))
        end
        if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Inventory") then
            game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory.Position = (_G.BackpackV2 == true and (_G.Backpack["New"]["Inventory"]) or (_G.Backpack["Old"]["Inventory"]))
        end
        for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:GetChildren()) do
            if v:IsA("TextButton") and v:FindFirstChild("Number") then
                v.Number.Position = (_G.BackpackV2 == true and (_G.Backpack["New"]["Backpack Number"][v.Name]) or (_G.Backpack["Old"]["Backpack Number"][v.Name]))
            end
        end
        if _G.BackpackV2 == true then
            if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Inventory").Visible == false then
                if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Hotbar"):FindFirstChild("UIListLayout") == nil then
                    local UIListLayout = Instance.new("UIListLayout")
                    UIListLayout.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Left
                    UIListLayout.Padding = UDim.new(0, 5)
                    UIListLayout.FillDirection = Enum.FillDirection.Horizontal
                    UIListLayout.HorizontalAlignment = Enum.HorizontalAlignment.Center
                    UIListLayout.VerticalAlignment = Enum.VerticalAlignment.Center
                    UIListLayout.Parent = game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar
                end
            else
                if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:FindFirstChild("UIListLayout") then
                    game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:FindFirstChild("UIListLayout"):Destroy()
                end
            end
            for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:GetChildren()) do
                if v:IsA("TextButton") then
                    if v:FindFirstChild("Equipped") then
                        v.Equipped.Visible = false
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("Equipped") and v:FindFirstChild("SelectionObjectClipper") then
                        v.SelectionObjectClipper.Visible = true
                    else
                        v.SelectionObjectClipper.Visible = false
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("UICorner") == nil then
                        local RobloxUi = Instance.new("UICorner", v)
                        RobloxUi.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
                    end
                end
            end
            for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory.ScrollingFrame.UIGridFrame:GetChildren()) do
                if v:IsA("TextButton") then
                    if v:FindFirstChild("Equipped") then
                        v.Equipped.Visible = false
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("Equipped") and v:FindFirstChild("SelectionObjectClipper") then
                        v.SelectionObjectClipper.Visible = true
                    else
                        v.SelectionObjectClipper.Visible = false
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("UICorner") == nil then
                        local RobloxUi = Instance.new("UICorner", v)
                        RobloxUi.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
                    end
                end
            end
            for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory:GetChildren()) do
                if v.Name == "Search" then
                    if v:FindFirstChild("UICorner") == nil then
                        local RobloxUi = Instance.new("UICorner", v)
                        RobloxUi.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("X") and v["X"]:FindFirstChild("UICorner") == nil then
                        local RobloxUi = Instance.new("UICorner", v["X"])
                        RobloxUi.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
                    end
                end
            end
            if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Inventory") and game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory:FindFirstChild("UICorner") == nil then
                local RobloxUi = Instance.new("UICorner", game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory)
                RobloxUi.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10)
            end
        elseif _G.BackpackV2 == false then
            if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:FindFirstChild("UIListLayout") then
                game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:FindFirstChild("UIListLayout"):Destroy()
            end
            for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:GetChildren()) do
                if v:IsA("TextButton") then
                    if v:FindFirstChild("Equipped") then
                        v.Equipped.Visible = true
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("SelectionObjectClipper") then
                        v.SelectionObjectClipper.Visible = false
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("UICorner") then
                        v:FindFirstChild("UICorner"):Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
            for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory.ScrollingFrame.UIGridFrame:GetChildren()) do
                if v:IsA("TextButton") then
                    if v:FindFirstChild("Equipped") then
                        v.Equipped.Visible = true
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("SelectionObjectClipper") then
                        v.SelectionObjectClipper.Visible = false
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("UICorner") then
                        v:FindFirstChild("UICorner"):Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
            for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory:GetChildren()) do
                if v.Name == "Search" then
                    if v:FindFirstChild("UICorner") then
                        v:FindFirstChild("UICorner"):Destroy()
                    end
                    if v:FindFirstChild("X") and v["X"]:FindFirstChild("UICorner") then
                        v["X"]:FindFirstChild("UICorner"):Destroy()
                    end
                end
            end
            if game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Inventory") and game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory:FindFirstChild("UICorner") then
                game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory:FindFirstChild("UICorner"):Destroy()
            end
        end
        task.wait()
    end
end)

-- Function for backpack slot interactions
local function BackpackV2(v)
    v.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
        if _G.BackpackV2 == true then
            local sound = Instance.new("Sound", workspace)
            sound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://10066942189"
            sound.Volume = 2
            sound.PlaybackSpeed = 1
            sound.PlayOnRemove = true
            sound:Destroy()
            game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v, TweenInfo.new(0.1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 70, 0, 70)}):Play()
        end
    end)
    v.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
        if _G.BackpackV2 == true then
            local sound = Instance.new("Sound", workspace)
            sound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://10066942189"
            sound.Volume = 2
            sound.PlaybackSpeed = 1
            sound.PlayOnRemove = true
            sound:Destroy()
            game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v, TweenInfo.new(0.1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 60)}):Play()
        end
    end)
    v.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if _G.BackpackV2 == true then
            local sound = Instance.new("Sound", workspace)
            sound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://10066936758"
            sound.Volume = 2
            sound.PlaybackSpeed = 1
            sound.PlayOnRemove = true
            sound:Destroy()
            local TweenGui = game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 70, 0, 70)})
            TweenGui:Play()
            TweenGui.Completed:Connect(function()
                game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(v, TweenInfo.new(0.1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {Size = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 60)}):Play()
            end)
        end
    end)
end

-- Apply to existing hotbar slots
for i, v in pairs(game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Hotbar:GetChildren()) do
    if v:IsA("TextButton") then
        BackpackV2(v)
    end
end

-- Apply to new slots when added
table.insert(_G.ConnectFun, game:GetService("CoreGui").RobloxGui.Backpack.Inventory.ScrollingFrame.UIGridFrame.ChildAdded:Connect(function(v)
    if v:IsA("TextButton") then
        BackpackV2(v)
    end
end))

        if Value then
            OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                Name = "Backpack V2",

                Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                Time = 2
            })
        else
-- do nothing
        end
    end
})

        -- No Hit Remote Gloves + Ignore Those Gloves
        ["Stilts"] = "",
        ["Glue"] = "",
        ["Spectator"] = "",

    -- Add metatable for dynamic glove lookups
    setmetatable(gloveHits, {
        __index = function(t, key)
            -- Try to find any remote that matches the glove name
            for _, child in pairs(ReplicatedStorage:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                    local childName = child.Name:lower()
                    local gloveName = tostring(key):lower()
                    
                    if childName == gloveName or
                       childName == gloveName .. "hit" or
                       childName == "ht" .. gloveName or
                       childName:find(gloveName, 1, true) then
                        rawset(t, key, child) -- Cache for next time
                        return child
                    end
                end
            end
            
            -- Ultimate fallback - first available remote
            for _, child in pairs(ReplicatedStorage:GetChildren()) do
                if child:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
                    rawset(t, key, child) -- Cache for next time
                    return child
                end
            end
            
            return nil
        end
    })
    
    -- Function to get current glove
    local function getCurrentGlove()
        local success, result = pcall(function()
            if localPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats") then
                local gloveValue = localPlayer.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove")
                if gloveValue then
                    return gloveValue.Value
                end
            end
            return "Default"
        end)
        
        if success then
            return result
        end
        return "Default"
    end
    
    -- Function to get the remote for a glove
    local function getGloveRemote(gloveName)
        -- Try direct lookup from gloveHits
        local remote = gloveHits[gloveName]
        
        if remote and typeof(remote) == "Instance" and remote:IsA("RemoteEvent") then
            return remote
        end
        
        -- If we get here, the metatable will handle it
        return gloveHits[gloveName]
    end
    
    -- Create slider
    local slapAuraSpeed = Tab:AddSlider({
        Name = "Slap Aura Speed",
        Min = 0.1,
        Max = 2,
        Default = 0.5,
        Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
        Increment = 0.1,
        ValueName = "seconds",
        Callback = function(Value)
            currentCooldown = Value
        end
    })
    
    -- Create toggle
    Tab:AddToggle({
        Name = "Slap Aura",
        Default = false,
        Callback = function(enabled)
            -- Prevent random "Slap Aura Disabled" popups
            if isSlapAuraEnabled == enabled then
                return
            end
            
            isSlapAuraEnabled = enabled
            
            if enabled then
                -- Disconnect existing connection
                if slapAuraConnection then
                    slapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnection = nil
                end
                
                -- Get current glove
                local currentGlove = getCurrentGlove()
                
                -- Get the remote for this glove
                local remote = getGloveRemote(currentGlove)
                
                if not remote then
                    OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                        Name = "Slap Aura Error",
                        Content = "No remote found for glove: " .. currentGlove,
                        Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                        Time = 3
                    })
                    isSlapAuraEnabled = false
                    return
                end
                
                print("Slap Aura: Enabled with glove '" .. currentGlove .. "' using remote '" .. remote.Name .. "'")
                
                -- Start slap aura
                slapAuraConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                    local currentTime = tick()
                    
                    -- Check cooldown
                    if currentTime - lastHitTime < currentCooldown then
                        return
                    end
                    
                    -- Check if still enabled and has character
                    if not isSlapAuraEnabled or not localPlayer.Character then
                        return
                    end
                    
                    -- Get local character position
                    local localChar = localPlayer.Character
                    local localRoot = localChar:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if not localRoot then
                        return
                    end
                    
                    -- Find players to slap
                    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                        if player ~= localPlayer and player.Character then
                            local char = player.Character
                            local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                            local torso = char:FindFirstChild("Torso") or char:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso")
                            
                            -- Check if valid target
                            if torso and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                -- Optional distance check (40 studs max)
                                local playerRoot = char:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                                if playerRoot then
                                    local distance = (playerRoot.Position - localRoot.Position).Magnitude
                                    if distance > 40 then
                                        continue
                                    end
                                end
                                
                                -- Fire the remote
                                local success, errorMsg = pcall(function()
                                    remote:FireServer(torso)
                                end)
                                
                                if success then
                                    lastHitTime = currentTime
                                    break -- Hit one player per cycle
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end)
                
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Slap Aura Enabled",
                    Content = "Glove: " .. currentGlove,
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 3
                })
                
            else
                -- Disable
                if slapAuraConnection then
                    slapAuraConnection:Disconnect()
                    slapAuraConnection = nil
                end
                
                -- Only show notification if it was previously enabled
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Slap Aura Disabled",
                    Content = "",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7733919105",
                    Time = 2
                })
            end
        end
    })
end

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Ghost Invisibility",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        local hasGhost = game.Players.LocalPlayer:FindFirstChild("leaderstats") and
                         game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats:FindFirstChild("Glove") and
                         game.Players.LocalPlayer.leaderstats.Glove.Value == "Ghost"

        if Value == true then
            if hasGhost then
                game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Ghostinvisibilityactivated:FireServer()
            else
                OrionLib:MakeNotification({
                    Name = "Error",
                    Content = "Equip Ghost Glove",
                    Image = "rbxassetid://7743878857",
                    Time = 3
                })
            end
        elseif Value == false and hasGhost then
            game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Ghostinvisibilitydeactivated:FireServer()
        end
    end
})

-- ServerHop (Regular Server)
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "ServerHop (Regular Server)",
    Callback = function()
        local PlaceID = game.PlaceId
        local AllIDs = {}
        local foundAnything = ""
        local actualHour = os.date("!*t").hour
        local Deleted = false

        local success, data = pcall(function()
            return game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONDecode(readfile("NotSameServers.json"))
        end)
        if success then
            AllIDs = data
        else
            table.insert(AllIDs, actualHour)
            writefile("NotSameServers.json", game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONEncode(AllIDs))
        end

        local function TPReturner()
            local Site
            if foundAnything == "" then
                Site = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. PlaceID .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100'))
            else
                Site = game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet('https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/' .. PlaceID .. '/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor=' .. foundAnything))
            end

            if Site.nextPageCursor and Site.nextPageCursor ~= "null" and Site.nextPageCursor ~= nil then
                foundAnything = Site.nextPageCursor
            end

            for i, v in pairs(Site.data) do
                local Possible = true
                local ID = tostring(v.id)
                if tonumber(v.maxPlayers) > tonumber(v.playing) then
                    for _, Existing in pairs(AllIDs) do
                        if ID == tostring(Existing) then
                            Possible = false
                            break
                        end
                    end
                    if Possible then
                        table.insert(AllIDs, ID)
                        wait()
                        pcall(function()
                            writefile("NotSameServers.json", game:GetService('HttpService'):JSONEncode(AllIDs))
                            wait()
                            game:GetService("TeleportService"):TeleportToPlaceInstance(PlaceID, ID, game.Players.LocalPlayer)
                        end)
                        wait(4)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
        end

        local function Teleport()
            while wait() do
                pcall(function()
                    TPReturner()
                    if foundAnything ~= "" then
                        TPReturner()
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

        -- Start teleporting to new servers
        Teleport()
    end
})

-- ServerHop (Small Server)
Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "ServerHop (Small Server)",
    Callback = function()
        local Http = game:GetService("HttpService")
        local TPS = game:GetService("TeleportService")
        local Api = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"
        local place = game.PlaceId
        local serversUrl = Api .. place .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"

        local function ListServers(cursor)
            local Raw = game:HttpGet(serversUrl .. ((cursor and "&cursor=" .. cursor) or ""))
            return Http:JSONDecode(Raw)
        end

        local Server, Next
        repeat
            local Servers = ListServers(Next)
            Server = Servers.data[1]
            Next = Servers.nextPageCursor
        until Server

        TPS:TeleportToPlaceInstance(place, Server.id, game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer)
    end
})

-- Auto Enter Arena System
local AutoEnterActive = false
local AutoEnterMode = "Arena" -- Default mode

Tab:AddDropdown({
    Name = "Enter",
    Default = "Arena",
    Options = {"Arena", "Arena Default"},
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoEnterMode = Value
    end
})

Tab:AddToggle({
    Name = "Auto Enter",
    Default = false,
    Callback = function(Value)
        AutoEnterActive = Value
        
        task.spawn(function()
            while AutoEnterActive do
                local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
                if not player then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local character = player.Character
                if not character or not character.Parent then 
                    task.wait(0.5) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if not hrp then 
                    task.wait(0.1) 
                    continue 
                end
                
                -- Check if already entered
                local entered = character:FindFirstChild("entered")
                
                if not entered then
                    -- Get the correct teleport part based on mode
                    local teleportFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Lobby")
                    if not teleportFolder then
                        task.wait(0.5)
                        continue
                    end
                    
                    local teleportPart = nil
                    
                    if AutoEnterMode == "Arena" then
                        teleportPart = teleportFolder:FindFirstChild("Teleport1")
                    elseif AutoEnterMode == "Arena Default" then
                        teleportPart = teleportFolder:FindFirstChild("Teleport2")
                    end
                    
                    if teleportPart then
                        pcall(function()
                            -- Method 1: Teleport player directly to the teleport part
                            local touchPart = nil
                            
                            -- Find the actual part to teleport to
                            if teleportPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                                touchPart = teleportPart
                            else
                                touchPart = teleportPart:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
                            end
                            
                            if touchPart then
                                -- Teleport player to the teleport location
                                hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                -- Move directly into the teleport part
                                hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                -- Spam teleport into the part to ensure trigger
                                for i = 1, 5 do
                                    hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame
                                    task.wait(0.01)
                                end
                                
                                -- Move slightly forward through the teleport
                                hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame + touchPart.CFrame.LookVector * 3
                                task.wait(0.1)
                                
                                -- Teleport back and forth through the teleport
                                for i = 1, 3 do
                                    hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame - touchPart.CFrame.LookVector * 2
                                    task.wait(0.05)
                                    hrp.CFrame = touchPart.CFrame + touchPart.CFrame.LookVector * 4
                                    task.wait(0.05)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                else
                    -- Already entered, just wait
                    task.wait(1)
                end
                
                -- Wait before next attempt
                task.wait(0.5)
            end
        end)
    end
})

Tab:AddButton({
    Name = "Teleport To Arena",
    Callback = function()
        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new()
        end
    end
})

    Name = "Teleport To Default Arena",
    Callback = function()
        local character = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
        if character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(122, 360, -3)
        end
    end
})
